This method will exceed device memory limits more often than second method since encrypting one large file versus many smaller files.  This method is always slower than second method.\r\n\r\nSecond method encrypts individual files located in hierarchy of AES folder.  This method is always faster than first method since folders are not archived into one file.    Folders of any size can be encrypted.
